/**
 * Number formatting symbols for locale aa.
 * @enum {string}
 */
goog.i18n.NumberFormatSymbols_aa = {
  DECIMAL_SEP: '.',
  GROUP_SEP: ',',
  PERCENT: '%',
  ZERO_DIGIT: '0',
  PLUS_SIGN: '+',
  MINUS_SIGN: '-',
  EXP_SYMBOL: 'E',
  PERMILL: '\u2030',
  INFINITY: '\u221E',
  NAN: 'NaN',
  DECIMAL_PATTERN: '#,##0.###',
  SCIENTIFIC_PATTERN: '#E0',
  PERCENT_PATTERN: '#,##0%',
  CURRENCY_PATTERN: '\u00A4#,##0.00',
  DEF_CURRENCY_CODE: 'DJF'
};

 * Number formatting symbols for locale en.
 * @enum {string}
 */
goog.i18n.NumberFormatSymbols_en = {
  DECIMAL_SEP: '.',
  GROUP_SEP: ',',
  PERCENT: '%',
  ZERO_DIGIT: '0',
  PLUS_SIGN: '+',
  MINUS_SIGN: '-',
  EXP_SYMBOL: 'E',
  PERMILL: '\u2030',
  INFINITY: '\u221E',
  NAN: 'NaN',
  DECIMAL_PATTERN: '#,##0.###',
  SCIENTIFIC_PATTERN: '#E0',
  PERCENT_PATTERN: '#,##0%',
  CURRENCY_PATTERN: '\u00A4#,##0.00;(\u00A4#,##0.00)',
  DEF_CURRENCY_CODE: 'USD'
};
